<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:opklaren.html>opklaren</a> (56405)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">up, on</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klaren.html>klaren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to (make/become) clear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opklaren.html>opklaren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To (make) clear(<a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a>), clarify</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To fix, solve (especially a riddle etc.)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> weather</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To become clear(<a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a>), to clear up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To (become) clear(<a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a>), clear up physically</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To clear up, to look, to feel etc. bright(<a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a>) etc.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To clear (up) oneself in either sense</li></ol>

***opknappen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:opknappen.html>opknappen</a> (5057)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knap.html>knap</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opknappen.html>opknappen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to overhaul, to renovate, to refurbish</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take care of (a job or task)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get better, to recuperate, to cheer up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Suriname" class="extiw" title="w:Suriname">Suriname</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to trounce</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">opknapbeurt</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:oploop.html>oploop</a></i>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:opmaken.html>opmaken</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maken.html>maken</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opmaken.html>opmaken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to use up (e.g. money) <i>or</i> eat up (all that's left to eat)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to finish, conclude</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make (a <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a>)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to put <a href = vnd.unilang:make-up.html>make-up</a> on</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> typography</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to format, to apply styling to</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to conclude, to infer [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></i> <span>(from)</span></span>]</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:opnaaien.html>opnaaien</a> (41778)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naaien.html>naaien</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sew</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opnaaien.html>opnaaien</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>rile up, provoke, excite
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">newspaper article header</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:eerst.html>Eerst</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:publiek.html>publiek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:opnaaien.html>opnaaien</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pakt.html>pakt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sagan.html>Sagan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:specialiteit.html>specialiteit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">First getting the spectators on their <a href = vnd.unilang:feet.html>feet</a> to then treat them to his signature move [namely a <a href = vnd.unilang:wheelie.html>wheelie</a>, editor's note]</span></dd></dl></div><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.hln.be/hln/nl/2444/Ronde-Van-Vlaanderen/article/detail/2665044/2016/04/03/Eerst-publiek-even-opnaaien-en-dan-pakt-Sagan-uit-met-specialiteit-van-het-huis.dhtml">[1]</a></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:carl.html>Carl</a> Hoefkens <a href = vnd.unilang:laat.html>laat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b>opnaaien‎</b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:carl.html>Carl</a> Hoefkens will not get himself <b>riled up</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sewing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To connect pieces by sewing them together.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:opname.html>opname</a> (3431)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Derived from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opnemen.html>opnemen</a></i> on the model of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Aufnahme</i>. The same <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> true of other nouns in <i>-name</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opname.html>opname</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opnamen.html>opnamen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opnames.html>opnames</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opname.html>opnametje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>The act of absorbing or assimilating, <span class="Latn" lang="en">uptake</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">absorption</span>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:opname.html>Opname</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:planten.html>planten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:algen.html>algen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:blijkt.html>blijkt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nemen.html>nemen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hogere.html>hogere</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:temperaturen.html>temperaturen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Absorption</b> by plants and algae appears to decrease at <a href = vnd.unilang:higher.html>higher</a> temperatures.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:absorptie.html>absorptie</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">recording</span>, a record, something that <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> recorded.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">In <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kast.html>kast</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voormalige.html>voormalige</a> studio <a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:opnames.html>opnames</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gevonden.html>gevonden</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A few more <b>recordings</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> found in a closet at the former studio.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>The act of recording.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tijdens.html>Tijdens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:opname.html>opname</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:mag.html>mag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niemand.html>niemand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:binnen.html>binnen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Nobody may go inside during a <b>recordings</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>The act of including, adopting or assimilating.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:opname.html>opname</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> geherintroduceerde <a href = vnd.unilang:soortgenoten.html>soortgenoten</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groep.html>groep</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ging.html>ging</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:soepeler.html>soepeler</a> than <a href = vnd.unilang:verwacht.html>verwacht</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b>adoption</b> of reintroduced members of the same species into the group when more smoothly than <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> expected.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>An intake, admission <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">for medical services</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">In <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koude.html>koude</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:streek.html>streek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pieken.html>pieken</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:opnames.html>opnames</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> winter.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Medical <a href = vnd.unilang:intakes.html>intakes</a></b> peak in winter in this cold region.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>The department or office in a medical facility (such a hospital) dealing with the admission of patients.</li></ol>

***opnemen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:opnemen.html>opnemen</a> (1695)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">opnēmen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nemen.html>nemen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opnemen.html>opnemen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pick up, to raise
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nam.html>nam</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:glas.html>glas</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sloeg.html>sloeg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:achterover.html>achterover</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She <b>raised</b> the glass and downed it.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pick up or answer (the phone or horn)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>Wie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:telefoon.html>telefoon</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:opnemen.html>opnemen</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> going to <b>answer</b>/<b>pick up</b> the phone.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

***opossum.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:opossum.html>opossum</a> (48762)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:opossum.html>opossum</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Powhatan_language" class="extiw" title="w:Powhatan language">Powhatan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pim">aposoum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">white animal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Algonquian" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Algonquian">Proto-Algonquian</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="alg-pro">*wa·p-aʔθemwa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">white dog</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***oppikken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:oppikken.html>oppikken</a> (5307)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pikken.html>pikken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oppikken.html>oppikken</a></strong>

***opportunist.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:opportunist.html>opportunist</a> (28029)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">opportuniste</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:opportunist.html>opportunist</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">opportunists</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Someone who <a href = vnd.unilang:takes.html>takes</a> advantage of any opportunity to advance their own situation, placing expediency above principle.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b> November 12,  “International friendly: England 1-0 Spain”, in  <cite>BBC Sport</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport2/hi/football/15693231.stm">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">James Milner's angled free-kick <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> headed on to the post by the tireless <a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>Bent</a> and Lampard the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:opportunist.html>opportunist</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> perfectly placed to <a href = vnd.unilang:stuipen.html>stoop</a> and head in from virtually on the goal-line.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">chancer</span></li></ul>

***oppositie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:oppositie.html>oppositie</a> (17608)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">opposicie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">oposicion</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">oppositio</i>, translating Ancient Greek <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀντίθεσις</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">antíthesis</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from the past participle <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> of classical <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">oppōnere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to set against</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oppositie.html>oppositie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oppositie.html>opposities</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oppositie.html>oppositietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>parliamentary <span class="Latn" lang="en">opposition</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">non-government factions in parliament</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">opposition</span>, resistance
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tegenstand.html>tegenstand</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verzet.html>verzet</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">up, <a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raken.html>raken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to reach</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***oprijlaan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:oprijlaan.html>oprijlaan</a> (22755)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">oprijden</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laan.html>laan</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oprijlaan.html>oprijlaan</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oprijlanen.html>oprijlanen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oprijlaan.html>oprijlaantje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>driveway</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oprit.html>oprit</a></i> and <i><a href = vnd.unilang:oprijlaan.html>oprijlaan</a></i> have almost the same meaning, but the latter <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used only for relatively long, wide and / or grand driveways, such as those leading to a palace or mansion.
</p>
